● Reading lower.c confirms the concrete blocker, and it's worth stating
  precisely rather than flailing: lowering doesn't just read CST structure — it
  reads semantic-derived facts like ls->is_type_alias (set by semantic) and
  resolved types. So lower-on-CST can't move independently; semantic must first
  put all the facts lower needs into the side model (today it carries only
  types). That makes 4d + S5 a coupled migration — semantic and lower move
  together, against an expanded side model — not two independent steps.

  So here's the honest landing point for this run:

  Built and verified (green throughout): the entire new front-end infrastructure
   —
  - lossless CST (S1 gates + S2 structural completeness),
  - typed view layer + global node-id space (S3),
  - semantic side-model channel, load-bearing in lowering (S4a/b),
  - CST-driven formatter PoC, idempotent over the corpus (S7).

  The compiler emits byte-identical code; decisions are in docs/LOSSLESS_CST.md.

  What remains is one coupled rewrite, not safely chunkable smaller: expand the
  side model to hold every semantic fact (types, is_type_alias, symbols),
  rewrite semantic to walk the CST and populate it, rewrite lower to consume CST
   + side model, then delete Program. The safe way is alongside-build → validate
   IR-identical on goldens + full corpus → switch — which is a large focused
  effort, genuinely multi-session, and the one place a mistake silently
  miscompiles.

  I'm not going to half-write that coupled rewrite and hand you a broken type
  checker — that'd be worse than the clean, fully-green, well-documented
  milestone we're at. The infrastructure it needs is now all in place, which is
  the hard, novel part. When you want, I pick up exactly there: side-model
  expansion first, then the alongside semantic+lower rewrite.

      787 +/* malloc'd NUL-terminated copy of a view's source text. */   
      788 +static char *cv_dup(CstView v) {                              
      789 +  CvText t = cv_text(v);                                      
      790 +  char *s = malloc(t.len + 1);                                
      791 +  if (t.ptr)                                                  
      792 +    memcpy(s, t.ptr, t.len);                                  
      793 +  s[t.len] = '\0';                                            
      794 +  return s;                                                   
      795 +}                                                             
      796 +                                                              
      797 +/* malloc'd NUL-terminated copy of a borrowed text slice. */  
      798 +static char *txt_dup(CvText t) {                              
      799 +  char *s = malloc(t.len + 1);                                
      800 +  if (t.ptr)                                                  
      801 +    memcpy(s, t.ptr, t.len);                                  
      802 +  s[t.len] = '\0';                                            
      803 +  return s;                                                   
      804 +}

      806 +/* Lower a CST type node (SN_TYPE_*) to an AstType, mirroring 
          +lower_type_ref. */                                            
      807 +static AstType *lower_type_cst(CstView t) {                   
      808 +  if (!cv_present(t))                                         
      809 +    return NULL;                                              
      810 +  AstType *at = ast_type_create(AST_TYPE_UNKNOWN);            
      811 +  switch (cv_kind(t)) {                                       
      812 +  case SN_TYPE_REF: {                                         
      813 +    CvText nm = cv_token(t, TOK_IDENT);                       
      814 +    char *name = txt_dup(nm);                                 
      815 +    if (strcmp(name, "archetype") == 0)                       
      816 +      at->tag = AST_TYPE_ARCHETYPE;                           
      817 +    else if (strcmp(name, "opaque") == 0)                     
      818 +      at->tag = AST_TYPE_OPAQUE;                              
      819 +    else if (strcmp(name, "type") == 0)                       
      820 +      ; /* meta-type erased; leave UNKNOWN defensively */     
      821 +    else                                                      
      822 +      *at = map_type_str(name); /* borrows name via AST_TYPE_N
          +AMED below */                                                 
      823 +    /* map_type_str's AST_TYPE_NAMED .name points at its argum
          +ent; keep a stable copy. */                                   
      824 +    if (at->tag == AST_TYPE_NAMED)                            
      825 +      at->name = name;                                        
      826 +    else                                                      
      827 +      free(name);                                             
      828 +    break;                                                    
      829 +  }                                                           
      830 +  case SN_TYPE_ARRAY: {                                       
      831 +    at->tag = AST_TYPE_ARRAY;                                 
      832 +    AstType *elem = ast_type_create(AST_TYPE_UNKNOWN);        
      833 +    char *en = txt_dup(cv_token(t, TOK_IDENT));               
      834 +    *elem = map_type_str(en);                                 
      835 +    if (elem->tag == AST_TYPE_NAMED)                          
      836 +      elem->name = en;                                        
      837 +    else                                                      
      838 +      free(en);                                               
      839 +    at->elem = elem;                                          
      840 +    break;                                                    
      841 +  }                                                           
      842 +  case SN_TYPE_SHAPED_ARRAY: {                                
      843 +    /* `T[a][b]...` — innermost element is the named type; eac
          +h `[n]` adds a rank.                                          
      844 +     * Reconstruct nested shaped arrays from the NUMBER tokens
          +. */                                                          
      845 +    char *en = txt_dup(cv_token(t, TOK_IDENT));               
      846 +    AstType *elem = ast_type_create(AST_TYPE_UNKNOWN);        
      847 +    *elem = map_type_str(en);                                 
      848 +    if (elem->tag == AST_TYPE_NAMED)                          
      849 +      elem->name = en;                                        
      850 +    else                                                      
      851 +      free(en);                                               
      852 +    /* collect ranks (NUMBER tokens) left-to-right */         
      853 +    int ranks[16], nr = 0;                                    
      854 +    for (int i = 0; i < t.node->child_count && nr < 16; i++)  
      855 +      if (t.node->children[i].tag == SE_TOKEN && t.node->child
          +ren[i].as.token.kind == TOK_NUMBER) {                         
      856 +        char buf[32];                                         
      857 +        int l = (int)t.node->children[i].as.token.length;     
      858 +        if (l > 31)                                           
      859 +          l = 31;                                             
      860 +        memcpy(buf, t.src + t.node->children[i].as.token.offse
          +t, l);                                                        
      861 +        buf[l] = '\0';                                        
      862 +        ranks[nr++] = atoi(buf);                              
      863 +      }                                                       
      864 +    AstType *cur = elem;                                      
      865 +    for (int i = nr - 1; i >= 0; i--) {                       
      866 +      AstType *sh = ast_type_create(AST_TYPE_SHAPED_ARRAY);   
      867 +      sh->elem = cur;                                         
      868 +      sh->rank = ranks[i];                                    
      869 +      cur = sh;                                               
      870 +    }                                                         
      871 +    free(at);                                                 
      872 +    return cur;                                               
      873 +  }                                                           
      874 +  case SN_TYPE_HANDLE: {                                      
      875 +    at->tag = AST_TYPE_HANDLE;                                
      876 +    /* handle<Name> / handle(Name): the archetype name is the 
          +second IDENT */                                               
      877 +    CvText h = cv_token(t, TOK_IDENT); /* "handle" */         
      878 +    (void)h;                                                  
      879 +    /* find the IDENT that isn't "handle" */                  
      880 +    for (int i = 0; i < t.node->child_count; i++)             
      881 +      if (t.node->children[i].tag == SE_TOKEN && t.node->child
          +ren[i].as.token.kind == TOK_IDENT) {                          
      882 +        CvText nm = {t.src + t.node->children[i].as.token.offs
          +et, t.node->children[i].as.token.length};                     
      883 +        if (!(nm.len == 6 && memcmp(nm.ptr, "handle", 6) == 0)
          +) {                                                           
      884 +          at->name = txt_dup(nm);                             
      885 +          break;                                              
      886 +        }                                                     
      887 +      }                                                       
      888 +    break;                                                    
      889 +  }                                                           
      890 +  default:                                                    
      891 +    break;                                                    
      892 +  }                                                           
      893 +  return at;                                                  
      894 +}

       896 +/* Resolved type of a CST expression node, from the side mode
           +l (keyed by node id). */                                     
       897 +static AstType cst_expr_type(CstView e) {                    
       898 +  return map_type_str(g_lower_model ? sem_model_expr_type(g_l
           +ower_model, cv_id(e)) : NULL);                               
       899 +}                                                            
       900 +                                                             
       901 +/* Decode a string token's content (quotes + escapes) like pa
           +rse_primary_expr does. */                                    
       902 +static char *cst_decode_string(CvText raw, int *out_len) {   
       903 +  const char *s = raw.ptr;                                   
       904 +  size_t len = raw.len;                                      
       905 +  char *value = malloc(len + 1);                             
       906 +  int p = 0;                                                 
       907 +  for (size_t i = 1; i + 1 < len; i++) {                     
       908 +    if (s[i] == '\\' && i + 2 < len) {                       
       909 +      i++;                                                   
       910 +      switch (s[i]) {                                        
       911 +      case 'n': value[p++] = '\n'; break;                    
       912 +      case 't': value[p++] = '\t'; break;                    
       913 +      case 'r': value[p++] = '\r'; break;                    
       914 +      case '\\': value[p++] = '\\'; break;                   
       915 +      case '"': value[p++] = '"'; break;                     
       916 +      default: value[p++] = s[i]; break;                     
       917 +      }                                                      
       918 +    } else {                                                 
       919 +      value[p++] = s[i];                                     
       920 +    }                                                        
       921 +  }                                                          
       922 +  value[p] = '\0';                                           
       923 +  *out_len = p;                                              
       924 +  return value;                                              
       925 +}                                                            
       926 +                                                             
       927 +/* The "innermost value expression" child of a node (skips ro
           +le-only name wrappers). */                                   
       928 +static CstView cst_first_expr(CstView v) {                   
       929 +  for (int i = 0; i < v.node->child_count; i++)              
       930 +    if (v.node->children[i].tag == SE_NODE) {                
       931 +      SyntaxNodeKind k = v.node->children[i].as.node->kind;  
       932 +      if (k >= SN_LITERAL_EXPR && k <= SN_PAREN_EXPR) {      
       933 +        CstView r = {v.node->children[i].as.node, v.src};    
       934 +        return r;                                            
       935 +      }                                                      
       936 +    }                                                        
       937 +  CstView none = {NULL, v.src};                              
       938 +  return none;                                               
       939 +}                                                            
       940 +                                                             
       941 +static AstExpr *lower_expr_cst(CstView e) {                  
       942 +  if (!cv_present(e))                                        
       943 +    return NULL;                                             
       944 +  AstExpr *ax = ast_expr_create(AST_EXPR_LITERAL);           
       945 +  ax->resolved = cst_expr_type(e);                           
       946 +                                                             
       947 +  switch (cv_kind(e)) {                                      
       948 +  case SN_PAREN_EXPR:                                        
       949 +    /* transparent: lower the inner expression */            
       950 +    return lower_expr_cst(cst_first_expr(e));                
       951 +  case SN_LITERAL_EXPR:                                      
       952 +    ax->kind = AST_EXPR_LITERAL;                             
       953 +    ax->data.literal.lexeme = cv_dup(e);                     
       954 +    break;                                                   
       955 +  case SN_STRING_EXPR: {                                     
       956 +    ax->kind = AST_EXPR_STRING;                              
       957 +    int n = 0;                                               
       958 +    ax->data.string.value = cst_decode_string(cv_text(e), &n)
           +;                                                            
       959 +    ax->data.string.length = n;                              
       960 +    break;                                                   
       961 +  }                                                          
       962 +  case SN_NAME_EXPR: {                                       
       963 +    ax->kind = AST_EXPR_NAME;                                
       964 +    /* table<Name> in value position resolves to the bare arc
           +hetype name */                                               
       965 +    if (cv_has_token(e, TOK_LT)) {                           
       966 +      /* second IDENT is the archetype name */               
       967 +      char *nm = NULL;                                       
       968 +      int seen = 0;                                          
       969 +      for (int i = 0; i < e.node->child_count; i++)          
       970 +        if (e.node->children[i].tag == SE_TOKEN && e.node->ch
           +ildren[i].as.token.kind == TOK_IDENT) {                      
       971 +          CvText t = {e.src + e.node->children[i].as.token.of
           +fset, e.node->children[i].as.token.length};                  
       972 +          if (seen++) {                                      
       973 +            nm = txt_dup(t);                                 
       974 +            break;                                           
       975 +          }                                                  
       976 +        }                                                    
       977 +      ax->data.name.name = nm ? nm : cv_dup(e);              
       978 +      ax->data.name.is_table_ref = 1;                        
       979 +    } else {                                                 
       980 +      ax->data.name.name = txt_dup(cv_token(e, TOK_IDENT));  
       981 +    }                                                        
       982 +    break;                                                   
       983 +  }                                                          
       984 +  case SN_FIELD_EXPR: {                                      
       985 +    /* `base.f1.f2…[idx]` is flat under one node: base IDENT,
           + then (DOT FIELD_NAME)+,                                     
       986 +     * optionally a trailing `[indices]`. Rebuild the left-as
           +soc AST. */                                                  
       987 +    AstExpr *base = ast_expr_create(AST_EXPR_NAME);          
       988 +    base->data.name.name = txt_dup(cv_token(e, TOK_IDENT));  
       989 +    AstExpr *cur = base;                                     
       990 +    int nfields = cv_count(e, SN_FIELD_NAME);                
       991 +    for (int i = 0; i < nfields; i++) {                      
       992 +      AstExpr *f = ast_expr_create(AST_EXPR_FIELD);          
       993 +      f->data.field.base = cur;                              
       994 +      f->data.field.field_name = cv_dup(cv_child_at(e, SN_FIE
           +LD_NAME, i));                                                
       995 +      cur = f;                                               
       996 +    }                                                        
       997 +    /* trailing index over the final field */                
       998 +    if (cv_has_token(e, TOK_LBRACKET)) {                     
       999 +      AstExpr *idx = ast_expr_create(AST_EXPR_INDEX);        
      1000 +      idx->data.index.base = cur;                            
      1001 +      int ic = 0;                                            
      1002 +      for (int i = 0; i < e.node->child_count; i++)          
      1003 +        if (e.node->children[i].tag == SE_NODE) {            
      1004 +          SyntaxNodeKind k = e.node->children[i].as.node->kin
           +d;                                                           
      1005 +          if (k >= SN_LITERAL_EXPR && k <= SN_PAREN_EXPR)    
      1006 +            ic++;                                            
      1007 +        }                                                    
      1008 +      idx->data.index.indices = calloc(ic ? ic : 1, sizeof(As
           +tExpr *));                                                   
      1009 +      idx->data.index.index_count = 0;                       
      1010 +      for (int i = 0; i < e.node->child_count; i++)          
      1011 +        if (e.node->children[i].tag == SE_NODE) {            
      1012 +          SyntaxNodeKind k = e.node->children[i].as.node->kin
           +d;                                                           
      1013 +          if (k >= SN_LITERAL_EXPR && k <= SN_PAREN_EXPR) {  
      1014 +            CstView iv = {e.node->children[i].as.node, e.src}
           +;                                                            
      1015 +            idx->data.index.indices[idx->data.index.index_cou
           +nt++] = lower_expr_cst(iv);                                  
      1016 +          }                                                  
      1017 +        }                                                    
      1018 +      cur = idx;                                             
      1019 +    }                                                        
      1020 +    free(ax);                                                
      1021 +    cur->resolved = cst_expr_type(e);                        
      1022 +    return cur;                                              
      1023 +  }                                                          
      1024 +  case SN_INDEX_EXPR: {                                      
      1025 +    ax->kind = AST_EXPR_INDEX;                               
      1026 +    AstExpr *base = ast_expr_create(AST_EXPR_NAME);          
      1027 +    base->data.name.name = txt_dup(cv_token(e, TOK_IDENT));

      1099 +          ax->data.call.args[ax->data.call.arg_count++] = low

      1104 +  default:

      1109 +    break;                                                   
      1110 +  }                                                          
      1111 +  return ax;

      958 +static CstView cv_node_at_expr(CstView v, int idx) {          
      959 +  int c = 0;                                                  
      960 +  for (int i = 0; i < v.node->child_count; i++)               
      961 +    if (v.node->children[i].tag == SE_NODE) {                 
      962 +      SyntaxNodeKind k = v.node->children[i].as.node->kind;   
      963 +      if (k >= SN_LITERAL_EXPR && k <= SN_PAREN_EXPR) {       
      964 +        if (c == idx) {                                       
      965 +          CstView r = {v.node->children[i].as.node, v.src};   
      966 +          return r;                                           
      967 +        }                                                     
      968 +        c++;                                                  
      969 +      }                                                       
      970 +    }                                                         
      971 +  CstView none = {NULL, v.src};                               
      972 +  return none;

      1147 +/* Lower the statement-kind child nodes of `parent` into an A

      1148 +static AstStmt **cst_lower_body(CstView parent, int *out_coun
           +t) {                                                         
      1149 +  int n = 0;                                                 
      1150 +  for (int i = 0; i < parent.node->child_count; i++)         
      1151 +    if (parent.node->children[i].tag == SE_NODE) {           
      1152 +      SyntaxNodeKind k = parent.node->children[i].as.node->ki
           +nd;                                                          
      1153 +      if (k >= SN_BIND_STMT && k <= SN_EACH_FIELD_STMT)      
      1154 +        n++;                                                 
      1155 +    }                                                        
      1156 +  *out_count = n;                                            
      1157 +  if (n == 0)                                                
      1158 +    return NULL;                                             
      1159 +  AstStmt **out = calloc(n, sizeof(AstStmt *));              
      1160 +  int j = 0;                                                 
      1161 +  for (int i = 0; i < parent.node->child_count; i++)

           +nd;

           +t.src};                                                      
      1166 +        out[j++] = lower_stmt_cst(sv);                       
      1167 +      }                                                      
      1168 +    }                                                        
      1169 +  return out;                                                
      1170 +}

      1173 +  switch (k) {                                               
      1174 +  case TOK_PLUS_EQ: return OP_ADD;                           
      1175 +  case TOK_MINUS_EQ: return OP_SUB;                          
      1176 +  case TOK_STAR_EQ: return OP_MUL;                           
      1177 +  case TOK_SLASH_EQ: return OP_DIV;                          
      1178 +  default: return OP_NONE; /* plain `=` */                   
      1179 +  }

      1182 +static AstStmt *lower_stmt_cst(CstView s) {                  
      1183 +  AstStmt *as = ast_stmt_create(AST_STMT_EXPR);              
      1184 +                                                             
      1185 +  switch (cv_kind(s)) {                                      
      1186 +  case SN_BIND_STMT: {                                       
      1187 +    if (g_lower_model && sem_model_bind_alias(g_lower_model, 
           +cv_id(s))) {                                                 
      1188 +      as->kind = AST_STMT_EXPR;                              
      1189 +      AstExpr *zero = ast_expr_create(AST_EXPR_LITERAL);     
      1190 +      zero->data.literal.lexeme = malloc(2);                 
      1191 +      strcpy(zero->data.literal.lexeme, "0");                
      1192 +      as->data.expr_stmt.expr = zero;                        
      1193 +      break;                                                 
      1194 +    }                                                        
      1195 +    as->kind = AST_STMT_BIND;

      1198 +    as->data.bind_stmt.names = calloc(1, sizeof(char *));    
      1199 +    as->data.bind_stmt.names[0] = cv_dup(target);            
      1200 +    as->data.bind_stmt.type = lower_type_cst(cv_child(s, SN_T
           +YPE_REF));

           +(s, 1));                                                     
      1202 +    break;                                                   
      1203 +  }                                                          
      1204 +  case SN_ASSIGN_STMT: {                                     
      1205 +    as->kind = AST_STMT_ASSIGN;                              
      1206 +    for (int i = 0; i < s.node->child_count; i++)            
      1207 +      if (s.node->children[i].tag == SE_TOKEN) {

           +NUS_EQ || tk == TOK_STAR_EQ ||                               
      1210 +            tk == TOK_SLASH_EQ) {

      1212 +          break;                                             
      1213 +        }                                                    
      1214 +      }                                                      
      1215 +    as->data.assign_stmt.target = lower_expr_cst(cv_node_at_e
           +xpr(s, 0));

           +pr(s, 1));                                                   
      1217 +    break;                                                   
      1218 +  }                                                          
      1219 +  case SN_EXPR_STMT:

      1221 +    as->data.expr_stmt.expr = lower_expr_cst(cv_node_at_expr(
           +s, 0));

      1412 +/* CST-driven entry, gated by ARCHE_LOWER_CST (validated agai
           +nst the IR goldens). */                                      
      1413 +AstProgram *lower_cst_to_ast_v2(const SyntaxNode *root, const
           + char *src) {                                                
      1414 +  if (!root)

      957 +/* nth direct child node that is a type form (SN_TYPE_REF/ARRA
          +Y/SHAPED/TUPLE/HANDLE). */                                    
      958 +static CstView cv_type_at(CstView v, int idx) {               
      959 +  int c = 0;                                                  
      960 +  for (int i = 0; i < v.node->child_count; i++)               
      961 +    if (v.node->children[i].tag == SE_NODE) {                 
      962 +      SyntaxNodeKind k = v.node->children[i].as.node->kind;   
      963 +      if (k >= SN_TYPE_REF && k <= SN_TYPE_HANDLE) {          
      964 +        if (c == idx) {                                       
      965 +          CstView r = {v.node->children[i].as.node, v.src};   
      966 +          return r;                                           
      967 +        }                                                     
      968 +        c++;                                                  
      969 +      }                                                       
      970 +    }                                                         
      971 +  CstView none = {NULL, v.src};                               
      972 +  return none;                                                
      973 +}                                                             
      974 +                                                              
      975 +static int cv_type_count(CstView v) {                         
      976 +  int c = 0;                                                  
      977 +  for (int i = 0; i < v.node->child_count; i++)               
      978 +    if (v.node->children[i].tag == SE_NODE) {                 
      979 +      SyntaxNodeKind k = v.node->children[i].as.node->kind;   
      980 +      if (k >= SN_TYPE_REF && k <= SN_TYPE_HANDLE)            
      981 +        c++;                                                  
      982 +    }                                                         
      983 +  return c;                                                   
      984 +}                                                             
      985 +

● Concrete, demonstrated state for this run:

  The CST-driven lowerer works end-to-end. Built lower_cst_to_ast_v2 (reads the
  CST + side model), gated by ARCHE_LOWER_CST so the default stays
  byte-identical. 3/10 codegen goldens are now IR-identical through the full 
  compiler via the CST path (simple, with_params, hello_world) — the approach
  and the whole infrastructure stack (CST → views → ids → side model → alias
  resolution) are proven, not theoretical.

  The gate found and I fixed three real couplings: type lookups must accept any
  type form (not just SN_TYPE_REF); nominal aliases (file→opaque) need
  semantic_resolve_type_alias; and the CST must be kept alive through lowering
  (main.c freed it after parse).

  Everything default-green: parser 47 · semantic 37 · codegen 8 · lower 7 · 
  cst-view 13 · verify-cst 292/292 · verify-codegen identical.

  The remaining diffs are specific, identified constructs (next:
  static-allocation capacity — codegen lays out the archetype struct from it, so
   it's a fact that must thread through, not just AST shape; then tuple
  flattening, modules). That capacity finding is the useful kind: it shows the
  last mile of the migration is the iterative gate-driven porting I'm already
  doing, with the oracle catching each gap.

  I'll keep grinding the same way — port the next construct, re-diff, repeat —
  and pull the trigger to make the CST path default + delete the Program-based
  lower once it's 10/10.
